<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:купить.html>купи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li>to reimburse, to pay back, to compensate (expenses)</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окупиться.html>окупи́ться</a> (28304)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окупить.html>окупи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окупиться.html>окупи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okupítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">окупа́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be reimbursed</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pay off, to be worth it in the end <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of difficulties, hardships, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окупить.html>окупи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***окутать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окутать.html>оку́тать</a> (10242)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ку́тать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окутать.html>оку́тать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okútatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окутывать.html>оку́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wrap <i>(round)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:окутать.html>оку́тать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шея.html>ше́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шарф.html>ша́рфом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okútatʹ</b> šéju šárfom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wrap a scarf round one's neck</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cloak <i>(in)</i>, to shroud <i>(in)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:окутанный.html>оку́танный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тайна.html>та́йной</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okútannyj</b> tájnoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cloaked in mystery</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ку́тать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кутаться.html>ку́таться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kútatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окутывать.html>оку́тывать</a> (18229)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окутать.html>оку́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окутывать.html>оку́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okútyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окутать.html>оку́тать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wrap <i>(round)</i></li>
<li>to cloak <i>(in)</i>, to shroud <i>(in)</i></li></ol>

***олень.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:олень.html>олень</a> (3004)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*(j)elenь</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁el-(h₁)en-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">red deer, elk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁el-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">red deer, elk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">elk</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἑλλός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hellós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">deer-calf</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἔλαφος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">élaphos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">deer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">elnias</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Armenian" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Armenian">Old Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="xcl">եղն</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xcl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ełn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:олень.html>оле́нь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">olénʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:олень.html>оле́ня</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:олень.html>оле́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:олень.html>оле́ней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>deer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:северный.html>се́верный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:олень.html>оле́нь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sévernyj <b>olénʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">reindeer</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американский.html>америка́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:северный.html>се́верный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:олень.html>оле́нь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">amerikánskij sévernyj <b>olénʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">caribou</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">безро́гий <b><a href = vnd.unilang:олень.html>оле́нь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bezrógij <b>olénʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">pollard</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благородный.html>благоро́дный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:олень.html>оле́нь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">blagoródnyj <b>olénʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">stag, red deer, elk (U.S.) (Cervus elaphus)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:олень.html>оле́нь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nastojáščij <b>olénʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">stag, red deer, elk (U.S.) (Cervus elaphus)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>buck, stag <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">male deer</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dimwit, fool, narrow-minded individual</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оливье.html>оливье́</a> (26918)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> given name <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">Olivier</i>,
named after Russian chef of Belgian origin <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lucien_Olivier" class="extiw" title="w:Lucien Olivier"><span class="None" lang="ru">Lucien Olivier</span></a>, who invented it in the 1860s. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">олів'є́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">olivʺjé</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оловянный.html>оловя́нный</a> (14043)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">оловѧнꙑи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">olovęnyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">оловѣнꙑи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">olověnyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*olověnъ</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*olověnьnъ</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*olovo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ěnъ</i>.
</p>

***олух.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>олух</a> (22535)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>о́лух</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ólux</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:олух.html>о́луха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:олух.html>о́лухи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:олух.html>о́лухов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>blockhead, dimwit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">stupid person</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:омар.html>ома́р</a> (14506)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
